After you check in, you can rent a cabinet with your room card and you can use it until you check out. (If you haven‚Äôt used up your ski rights, you can still use them on the day after check-out)

There is also a swimming pool on the first floor, an entertainment hall for shooting, catching dolls, billiards, etc., but the outdoor soup pool requires an additional fee. The water for washing hands in the bathroom in the lobby on the first floor is too cold. It is recommended to use warm water.

There are buses from Jilin Railway Station and Changchun Airport to Vanke Songhua Lake Ski Resort. Just check the schedule and book the itinerary.

I am very satisfied with my stay at Seibu Prince Hotel. I will come back next time.

msg:First of all, because I like Seibu Prince Hotel in Songhua Lake, I chose to come to Vanke Songhua Lake for vacation with my friends during the holidays. But the accommodation experience this time was very unsatisfactory. On the contrary, the leisurely stroll in Qingshan made us relax.

1. There is no exhaust in the bathroom, no non-slip slippers in the bathroom, and the anti-slip mat is very small. After taking a bath, the ground is full of water. After wearing it, the water still doesn‚Äôt go down. You can only wear hotel slippers to open the window for ventilation. Be very careful during the whole process. Because it is very easy to slip and there are serious safety hazards, it is recommended that the hotel not provide anti-slip slippers but lay anti-slip mats.

2. The scenery outside the window is very good. The color scheme of the villa area and the green mountains are really beautiful. I was very happy at first, but when I took pictures, I found that the window glass was dirty and there were many mud spots, which affected the perception of the scenery.

3. The air conditioner is very cold when sleeping at night and very hot during the day, and the operation button prompts are not obvious, resulting in a dry room, and there are remaining flocs and cloudy liquid in the humidifier, which cannot be used. I didn't call the room service staff to clean it up late at night, so I had to drink plenty of water by myself, so I woke up frequently and couldn't sleep well at night. I found bloodshot eyes when I washed my face and blown my nose in the morning.

4. There is no food in the off-season breakfast, only text menus, portions and ingredients, it is recommended to match pictures, and ask about taboos to avoid waste.

5. When I came out of the restaurant, I didn‚Äôt see the restroom. I asked the lady in uniform who looked like a cleaning lady of the hotel (the hotel later explained that this person was not an internal staff member of the hotel). She was only 20 meters away from the restroom, but she directed guests to the public restroom 200 meters away from the hotel. .

6. There are apples in the welcome fruit. When I bit them open, I found white wriggling worms in them, which made my friends sick for a long time. It is not the hotel's fault that this kind of thing happened, but just in case, it is recommended to replace it with fruits that do not grow worms.

7. The color of the bathtub water is yellow, which can‚Äôt be solved even after contacting it many times. It may be that the water in the off-season is low and cannot be fully circulated. If the soft water system cannot be used, it is recommended that the hotel use a soft water faucet with a filter element.

advantage:
1. Xiaoguo at the front desk and several room service staff respond in a timely manner and can provide help when needed. Although some problems have not been substantively resolved (such as water quality, non-slip slippers), but the service attitude is worthy of praise.

2. The hotel environment is very good, the coffee shop is clean, warm and bright, the drinks are good, and the young lady speaks softly and sincerely.

3. After checking in, you can take the cable car to the top of the mountain for sightseeing. There are very few people in the off-season now, so you don‚Äôt have to queue for anything, and the air is very good.

I sincerely hope that the supporting facilities and details can be improved!

all of above
